96319 The Amarr Empire has had its share of religious cults and fanatics in the past, but few have been as successful, or as highly feared, as the Blood Raiders. The Blood Raiders are a sect of an ancient cult called Sani Sabik, who use blood in their rituals. The Blood Raiders believe that cloned bodies have "purer" blood than other bodies, and this explains while they operate mainly in space, attacking unwary spacefarers and draining their bodies of blood. The Blood Raiders are led by the fearsome Omir Sarikusa, who has remained on top of the DED's most wanted list for many years now. Under Sarikusa's leadership, the Blood Raiders have become more organized, establishing several bases in the Bleak Lands region. 140742 The Reclaiming is a major part of the Amarr religion, and of the Empire itself. They believe that all people in the universe were once part of the same empire, and the Amarr Empire is the direct heir to that legacy. Through Empress Jamyl Sarum the Amarr are given a divine mandate to reunify the peoples of the universe through any means necessary.


Historically, this has lead to numerous wars of conquest in which the Amarr decimate and then absorb civilizations. Each war is itself referred to as a Reclaiming to emphasize their divine mandate.

Warp to the Caldari Monument
The story of the Caldari begins with Caldari Prime, a cold world at the outer edge of the Luminaire system's habitable zone. From Caldari Prime the Civire and Deteis people formed a civilization was the precursor to the modern Caldari State. The Caldari shared their home system with the nearby Gallente Prime, and the Caldari were founding members of the Federated Union of Gallente Prime in BYC115. The Caldari never wholly clicked with Gallente government however and the two planets would slowly grow apart politically.		 <url=showinfo:5//30004967>Luminaire</url>: Caldari Monument

Warp to the Landfall Kutuoto Miru Orbital Center
To preserve the Caldari cultural identity and autonomy within the stifling Gallente Federation, Caldari megacorporations began establishing Caldari colonies outside of Federation authority, including the founding of Landfall City in the system that would become known as New Caldari. Many of these early colonies are now prominent planets within the modern Caldari State. When the Gallente learned of the colonies they demanded they be placed under Federation control, and this demand hurtled the Caldari and Gallente on a path towards secession and war.		 <url=showinfo:5//30000145>New Caldari</url>: Landfall Kutuoto Miru Orbital Center

When the Caldari seceded from the Federation, the Gallente waged a brutal war to prevent their independence. The war lasted nearly a century and was fought to a stalemate as the Caldari developed innovative technology like fighters and frigates to defend against their larger foe.
